.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf:

=============
CmpUserMgrItf
=============

.. contents::
    :local:
    :depth: 1

Interface of CmpUserMgr.

Detailed Description
--------------------

Interface for the user management component.

The user management in the runtime system is based on ACL (Access Control Lists). Here we have Users and UserGroups and access rights on objects.

The user manager requires some other interfaces to be implemented for full functionality:

1. CmpUserDB: This interface contains the basic functions to authentica users and to upload users to the CODESYS IDE in order to manage Groups. This interface has only read access to the database. No functions that can changed a value are defined here. This is the first interface to start if there is an existing user management that should be used by the CODESYS runtime system.

2. CmpUserDBConfiguration: This interface is used by the UserManager to Change the content of the users database. If this is not implemented it is not possible to manage the users and the corresponding credentials using the CODESYS IDE.

3. CmpUserGroupsDB: This interface provides access to existing user groups and users inside groups. This interface is read only too. No changes to the database can be done using this interface.

4. CmpUserGroupsDBConfiguration: This interface allows to configure the user groups and allows to assign members to groups.

All of these four interfaces are defined as static interfaces. To allow the user manager to use these interfaces it is required that the implementing component / components register the desired backends to the CmpUserMgr. It is possible to replace only the User Authentication interface and to stay with the default user groups and right database. This allows easy adoption of the CODESYS runtime to existing user databases.

5. CmpUserObjectsDB:

Every object in the runtime system, that must be protected with access rights, is registered dynamically during startup of the runtime by the corresponding component under the appropriate folder.

The objects in the runtime system are organized as a tree with 2 root nodes:

  - Runtime system object: "Device" | "PlcLogic" | "Application" | "Logger" | "Settings" | "UserManagement"

  - File system objects: "/" | "Temp" | "Test.txt"

On every object there are assigned all user groups. And for every user group you can specify the appropriate access rights.

There are 5 different access rights that can be specified at every group for each object:

  - USERDB_RIGHT_NONE: Access denied

  - USERDB_RIGHT_VIEW: Only view rights on the object. Object cannot be modified in any case!

  - USERDB_RIGHT_MODIFY: Object can be viewed and modified

  - USERDB_RIGHT_EXECUTE: Object can be executed

  - USERDB_RIGHT_ADD_REMOVE: It is allowed to add and remove objects or sub objects

  - USERDB_RIGHT_ALL: All rights allowed on the object

Not every access right is retrieved by an object. Which access rights are used are specified by each object and are masked in the user rights editor in the programming system!

Function Documentation
----------------------

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga269ec4966911ecf4171586b0396dd9f3:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrRegisterUserDB (RTS_HANDLE hDatabase, RTS_UI32 type)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Register a user database to the user manager. Only one database can be registered. If not database is registred then the user management will be deactivated if allowed.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------+--------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDatabase | Handle to the database.                          |
+---------+-----------+--------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | type      | The credentials type that the database supports. |
+---------+-----------+--------------------------------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1gabc4880247829c42711edd31316faa97a:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrUnregisterUserDB (RTS_HANDLE hDatabase)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Unregister a user database from the user manager.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------+-------------------------+
| [in]    | hDatabase | Handle to the database. |
+---------+-----------+-------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1gabd70a957878a22ac509b699e9ffea3ce:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrRegisterUserDBConfig (RTS_HANDLE hDatabase, RTS_UI32 type)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Register a configuration database. If this interface is registered the online services can change the user database.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------+--------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hDatabase | Handle to the database.                          |
+---------+-----------+--------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | type      | The credentials type that the database supports. |
+---------+-----------+--------------------------------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga969ad6158dd2dd5afa8163411d6348ba:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrSelectAuthType (RTS_UI32 ui32ClientFlags, RTS_UI32 *pui32AuthType)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Selects the authentication type out of the client proposals. Only to be called by CmpDevice.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ui32ClientFlags | Flags describing the clients behavior during login                          |
+---------+-----------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [inout] | pui32AuthType   | In: Client proposed authentication type. Out: Selected authentication type. |
+---------+-----------------+-----------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

**Return values**

+-------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK            | Login was successful                                                       |
+-------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER     | pui32AuthType is NULL                                                      |
+-------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_TYPE_MISMATCH | Non of the proposed authentication types matches the runtime requirements. |
+-------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga637c970f8bc0a5157d4935fe66d66a50:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrHandleLoginService (RTS_UI32 SessionId, RTS_UI32 SessionAuthType, RTS_UI32 SessionFlags, BINTAGWRITER *pWriter, BINTAGREADER *pReader, RTS_HANDLE *phUser)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Handles a UserMgr login request received by CmpDevice. Only to be called by CmpDevice.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------------+------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | SessionId       | SessionId of the device's online connection          |
+---------+-----------------+------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | SessionAuthType | Authentication algorithm used for the online session |
+---------+-----------------+------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | SessionFlags    | Flags describing the online session                  |
+---------+-----------------+------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pWriter         | Pointer the writer stream                            |
+---------+-----------------+------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pReader         | Pointer the reader stream                            |
+---------+-----------------+------------------------------------------------------+
| [out]   | phUser          | Pointer to return the user handle                    |
+---------+-----------------+------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

**Return values**

+----------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK               | Login was successful                                               |
+----------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PENDING          | Login is in progress, further online services needed.              |
+----------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER        | At least one of the parameters is NULL                             |
+----------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NO_ACCESS_RIGHTS | Login was denied e. g. because of wrong user/password combination. |
+----------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_TYPE_MISMATCH    | Authentication type does not match the negotiated type             |
+----------------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------+

^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Checks if the user management is active.

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga302a7c1de861d64ea2aae9d9aa3952aa:

RTS_HANDLE UserMgrLogin (char *pszUser, char *pszPassword, RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Logs user in to the runtime system using an active user management.

**Parameters**

+---------+-------------+-----------------------+
| [in]    | pszUser     | Name of the user      |
+---------+-------------+-----------------------+
| [in]    | pszPassword | Password (plain text) |
+---------+-------------+-----------------------+
| [out]   | pResult     | Pointer to error code |
+---------+-------------+-----------------------+

**Return values**

+-----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK                | User/password combination is valid                                                                          |
+-----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_ACTIVATE_USERMGMT | The login was successful. But the user management is enforced and not active. Activate the user management. |
+-----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_CHANGE_PASSWORD   | The login was successful. But the user must change his password.                                            |
+-----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NO_USERMGMT       | Login was not successful. The user management is not activated. Use empty user and password to login.       |
+-----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NO_ACCESS_RIGHTS  | The login was not successful, because of another reason.                                                    |
+-----------------------+-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Handle to the user or RTS_INVALID_HANDLE if not available

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga5d11a545de34d03cd0d6cc0f8e6733a4:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrHasAccessRights (char *pszObject, RTS_UI32 ulSessionId, RTS_UI32 ulRequestedRights)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Checks user access rights on the specified object (authorization)!

**Parameters**

+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszObject         | Full object name (see object tree)                                                          |
+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulSessionId       | SessionID of the device online connection (see :ref:`CmpDeviceItf.h <_cmp_device_itf_8h>` ) |
+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulRequestedRights | Requested rights on that object                                                             |
+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

**Return values**

+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK               | If user has the requested rights on the object or if no user management is configured |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER        | If SessionID or user is not available or the object does not exist                    |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_FAILED           | If something failed retrieving the access rights                                      |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NO_ACCESS_RIGHTS | Explicitly denied rights                                                              |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_INVALID_HANDLE   | Related user handle of the session is invalid or unknown                              |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga656e11e35075b93e09d2ca7a56967665:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrGetAccessRights (char *pszObject, RTS_UI32 ulSessionId, RTS_UI32 *pulRights, RTS_UI32 *pulDeniedRights)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Get user access rights on the specified object (authorization)!

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszObject       | Full object name (see object tree)                                                                                                                                                   |
+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulSessionId     | SessionID of the device online connection (see :ref:`CmpDeviceItf.h <_cmp_device_itf_8h>` )                                                                                          |
+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pulRights       | Pointer to get admitted rights                                                                                                                                                       |
+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pulDeniedRights | Pointer to get denied rights. NOTE: If the required right is denied _and_ admitted on the specified object, the denied right is more significant and so the access must be denied !! |
+---------+-----------------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

**Return values**

+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK               | If user has the requested rights on the object or if no user management is configured |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER        | If SessionID or user is not available or the object does not exist                    |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_FAILED           | If something failed retrieving the access rights                                      |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NO_ACCESS_RIGHTS | Explicitly denied rights                                                              |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_INVALID_HANDLE   | Related user handle of the session is invalid or unknown                              |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

RTS_RESULT UserMgrAddInfoToUser (RTS_HANDLE hUser, RTS_SIZE key, RTS_TYPEDVALUE *pValue)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Adds an value to an logged in user. This can be used as some kind of cache that exists as long as the user is logged in.

**Parameters**

+---------+--------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hUser  | Handle to the user.                                                                              |
+---------+--------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | key    | Access key for the cache value. This has to be used at UserMgrGetInfoOfUser to access the value. |
+---------+--------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pValue | Value to cache at the user.                                                                      |
+---------+--------+--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Return values**

+---------------+------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK        | Value cached                       |
+---------------+------------------------------------+
| ERR_DUPLICATE | The same key has been used already |
+---------------+------------------------------------+
| ERR_FAILED    | The caching failed                 |
+---------------+------------------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga086c3b0db90ac145d197f64c56c09810:

| ERR_OK        | Removing cache value successful         |

| ERR_NO_OBJECT | No cache value with this key available. |

| ERR_FAILED    | Removing cache value failed             |

RTS_RESULT UserMgrGroupAddUser (RTS_HANDLE hUser, char *pszGroupName, char *pszUserName)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Adds a user to a group in the user group database

**Parameters**

+---------+--------------+--------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hUser        | Handle of user with the appropriate rights |
+---------+--------------+--------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszGroupName | Name of the group.                         |
+---------+--------------+--------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszUserName  | Name of the user.                          |
+---------+--------------+--------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

**Return values**

+----------------------+---------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK               | User could be added                   |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER        | pszGroupName or pszUserName was NULL. |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------+
| ERR_NOMEMORY         | No memory to add user to group        |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------+
| ERR_DUPLICATE        | pszUserName is already added.         |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------+
| ERR_NO_ACCESS_RIGHTS | User has no access rights             |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------+

RTS_RESULT UserMgrAddOnlineAccessError (BINTAGWRITER *pWriter, RTS_RESULT Result, char *pszObject, RTS_UI32 ulRequestedRights, RTS_UI32 ulSessionID)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Adds the error tag to the reply stream of an online service, if the service is denied because of a failed access right (authorization error)!

**Parameters**

+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pWriter           | Pointer the writer stream                                                                   |
+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | Result            | Result code of the operation                                                                |
+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszObject         | Pointer to name of the object, whose access was denied                                      |
+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulRequestedRights | Requested rights on the object, which are not enabled                                       |
+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulSessionId       | SessionID of the device online connection (see :ref:`CmpDeviceItf.h <_cmp_device_itf_8h>` ) |
+---------+-------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

**Return values**

+------------+--------------------------------+
| ERR_OK     | Reply tag could be created     |
+------------+--------------------------------+
| ERR_FAILED | Reply tag could not be created |
+------------+--------------------------------+

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1gaa021567cec09ab6cc29943be279b432e:

RTS_HANDLE UserMgrObjectAdd (char *pszObject, RTS_RESULT *pResult)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Adds a new object to the user management, so the access rights can be configured on that object. NOTE: The name of the object must include the full name-space with "Device" as the root node, e.g. "Device.MyObject" or if it's a file system object with "/" as the root node.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------+------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszObject | Full object name (see object tree) |
+---------+-----------+------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult   | Pointer to error code              |
+---------+-----------+------------------------------------+

**Return values**

+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK             | Object could be added                                          |
+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER      | Object invalid = NULL or empty                                 |
+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NOTINITIALIZED | The user management is not initialized or it is not loaded yet |
+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NOMEMORY       | If memory could not be allocated to store this object          |
+--------------------+----------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Handle to the object or RTS_INVALID_HANDLE if it could not be added

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga363c3413dc5373024db05ce129bd3eb1:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrObjectSetUsedRights (RTS_HANDLE hObject, RTS_UI32 ulUsedRights)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Sets the used access rights for the object specified by handle. The rights are additionally stored in an internal list. In case USERDB_RIGHT_NONE is passed for ulUsedRights the previously stored rights are retrieved for this object.

**Parameters**

+---------+--------------+-------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hObject      | Handle to the object                                  |
+---------+--------------+-------------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | ulUsedRights | Used access rights or USERDB_RIGHT_NONE for retrieval |
+---------+--------------+-------------------------------------------------------+

**Return values**

+---------------+-------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK        | Rights are successfully set               |
+---------------+-------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER | Invalid object handle                     |
+---------------+-------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NO_OBJECT | Object was not found for rights retrieval |
+---------------+-------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1gae57cc6e510589eb43c49d6787185e716:

**Return values**

+---------------+------------------------------------------+
| ERR_OK        | Rights are successfully set              |
+---------------+------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER | Invalid object handle or invalid pointer |
+---------------+------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1ga53c3ea3e0dfae31bd085371b11caa6d5:

Opens an existing object. Checks if the user is member of at least one group that has access to this object.

**Parameters**

+---------+-----------+------------------------------------+
| [in]    | pszObject | Full object name (see object tree) |
+---------+-----------+------------------------------------+
| [in]    | hUser     | Handle of the logged in user.      |
+---------+-----------+------------------------------------+
| [out]   | pResult   | Pointer to error code              |
+---------+-----------+------------------------------------+

+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+

+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_PARAMETER        | Object not available of invalid.                              |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+
| ERR_NO_ACCESS_RIGHTS | User has no access rights to this object.                     |
+----------------------+---------------------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Handle to the object or RTS_INVALID_HANDLE if it is not available or no access rights are existing.

.. _group___cmp_user_mgr_itf_1gacbebe1eb0e031d30ed2cd8b74b602a54:

RTS_RESULT UserMgrAnnounceOldDatabase (RTS_UI32 info)
^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^

Tells the UserManager that there is an old format database found: The announcement ANNOUNCE may return an error other than ERR_OK (ERR_OPERATION_DENIED is recommended) which indicates that the conversion of the old database is denied. The announcement FINISH tells the UserManager that an old database is converted and adjustment may be processed now.

**Parameters**

+---------+------+--------------------------------------------------+
| [in]    | info | ANNOUNCE, FINISH, see Old database announcements |
+---------+------+--------------------------------------------------+

**Returns:**

Error code

**Return values**

+--------+-----------+
| ERR_OK | Succeeded |
+--------+-----------+
